Test Location- Chaos Objects
Test Location- Character 
This can be referenced by other objects to check the state of the chain%2C if you want.
This cuts the nav mesh during the cutscene. Place this over any areas you don%27t want NPCs to wander into during the cutscene. It must be completely enclosed within the DespawnVolume%2C otherwise you might get characters stuck on cut nav mesh. If this isn%27t needed%2C uncheck it.
This has to be added to turn off the green lights even though they%27re set disabled - I believe because vehicles force enable all their children.
This objective reports the state of the object%3A%0Adeactivated %3D maglocked shut.%0Aactivated %3D maglocks open%2C ready to be destroyed.%0Acompleted %3D destroyed.%0AUse conditionals under the objective to control clamping.%0ACheck the %22persistent_state%22 box if you%27d like to persist destruction.

wcorprp
we never complete this objective directly - instead the parent-parent objective %28module main objective%29 will complete when the correct vehicle is in the scanner. The reason why that logic is there is to allow for a target vehicle to be placed in the scanner at any time and complete the objective%2C even before the player is told to do so.
